Compared with the noisy and chaotic old street across the bridge outside the scenic area, this place can be said to be a paradise. The green coverage area is large and the sense of hierarchy is strong. There are many projects for children to play: children's playground, sand pool, rowing boat, kayak, handmade rice cake, batik... In addition to the convenience of sightseeing and playing, the most commendable thing about the entire hotel is the service. At first, I felt that it was a bit inconvenient to need a shuttle bus from the lobby to the room. But the shuttle bus quickly "arrived" every time and quickly dispelled my concerns. Booked two rooms, checked in one first, and the front desk contacted the other one as soon as it was cleaned and sent the room card to the room; no matter which staff member I asked, I could get a warm and detailed answer, and even gave good suggestions; the front desk responded quickly when I bought toiletries; I asked the restaurant staff about watching the musical fountain in the evening, and in addition to being told the specific time of the start, I also knew where the best viewing point was; I didn't have to go to the lobby to check out, I could hand it over to any shuttle bus driver or even other staff. They would also take the initiative to show the parking picture to waive the parking fee. The only regret I felt was that the bathroom in the public area needed to be cleaned better. msg:There were three of us and we booked a family room in this resort to spend the weekend in Gaochun.
The layout of the resort and the scenery of the park are very good. The scenery you see after entering the lobby is so beautiful. At dusk, watching the sunset is also very attractive. The family room is clean and spacious, the bathroom has both shower and bath, and there is also a small outdoor garden, making it feel comfortable.

But the service and some hospitality details need to be improved.

1. Clear instructions should be given to the guests: Check in at the counter, and after giving the room card, they did not explain anything. They only asked us to go to another counter near the window to go through the facial recognition procedure for entering the park. After completing it, That's all. Then we looked at the room card number, dragged our luggage and my mother back and forth in the lobby to find the room. We couldn't find it, so we went back to the counter to ask. It turned out that because our room was in the park, we had to leave the lobby and walk out of the main entrance. Turn left and walk ~100 meters to the entrance of the park, enter the gate, go down to the first floor, and wait for the shuttle bus to take passengers to the room. Oh my God! The way to the room was roundabout. Why did the waiters at the two counters not give any instructions or simple diagrams when checking in? Was it a "treasure hunt" for first-time guests?
In addition, there were no employees at the place where we were waiting for the shuttle bus, and there were no signboards. We didn‚Äôt know when the bus would be available, and we didn‚Äôt know if we were waiting at the correct place.
2. Housekeeping shortcomings:
After much tossing, we finally got to the room. I realized that some items in the room were not enough for 3 adults, so I called the front desk and asked for an extra teacup and a quilt. The answer I got was that they didn't have an extra teacup, so they arranged for paper cups to be sent to the room for us. It's really strange that a slightly larger hotel doesn't have an extra teacup. As for the quilt, there is a backup quilt in the closet. We are asked to look for it. If we can't find it, we can ask the housekeeper who brought the paper cup to help us find it. Okay, I tried to find it to no avail, so I have to wait for the housekeeper to arrive.
After waiting for half an hour, we called the front desk again. They seemed to have never received the request before, so we had to ask again. This time, after waiting for about 20 minutes, the housekeeper finally came with a paper cup. I searched for the quilt for a long time, and even lifted the mattress to see if there was anything under the bedüò∞. The result was that I found it in the small cabinet next to the small refrigerator and under the water cup. A "treasure hunt"!
3. Hotel information: From the lobby to the room, I don‚Äôt see many icons introducing the facilities in the park. I don‚Äôt know where my room is in the park, and I don‚Äôt know where the food, shopping, entertainment, etc. are. Another "treasure hunt". It turned out that there was a fireworks show by the lake in front of Chunqiu Pavilion in the evening, and I was only lucky enough to see it when I happened to have dinner at a nearby restaurant.
4. Disappoin**ent in crab restaurants: I went to Gaochun in November and wanted to try fresh steamed hairy crabs. I finally found out that there is a "crab restaurant" in the hotel, so I thought they would be good for eating crabs, but... steamed The maximum price is only 3 ‰°°, and the drunken crab is only 5 ‰°° (maybe because the steamed crabs are fresh every day and not stored for a long time, so they don‚Äôt have them in stock). I ordered steamed crabs and the crabs were brought to the table. There were no scissors or other tools. I asked them for tools for eating hairy crabs, but it turned out that the restaurant didn‚Äôt have themü§¶üèª‚ôÄ. I had to ask for vinegar before they remembered to provide it. The crab powder tofu had no crab powder taste and the steamed scallops were over steamed. It cost more than ¬•600 for 3 people, but they were all disappointed.

It is suggested that if there is any problem during the check-in process, it is best to communicate with the hotel in time, and the hotel can try to solve it well.

Before checking in, it is recommended to do a guide to understand the distribution of hotel rooms. The hotel is together with the Gucheng Bay Scenic Area, and some rooms are Located in the building where the lobby is located, another part of the guest rooms are scattered in the Gucheng Bay Scenic Area, which requires a shuttle bus from the scenic area, and the swimming pool is in the area where the lobby is located. If guests living in the scenic area want to swim, they must take the shuttle bus. It is not practical to take a shuttle bus (you have to take a shuttle bus in the middle) to go to the hotel lobby for a swim. After swimming, it is not practical to transfer the shuttle bus twice to the room, but there is no changing room and shower room on the first floor of the hotel. , so parents should bring their own clothes and towels and simply change their children's clothes in the bathroom in the hotel lobby, and then take the car back to the room in the scenic area to wash. Therefore, if you want to take your child to swim, it is best to book a room in the building where the hotel lobby is located, especially if you have a baby, so as not to fret. After all, the weather is so hot, and although the distance is not far, it is more painful to go back and forth for two shuttle buses.

If you ignore the problem of swimming, you can give full marks to hotel services and other aspects. Living in the scenic spot is inconvenient to swim, but the scenery is very good. If the weather is not hot, it is very comfortable to stroll in the scenic spot. It's not too tiring to walk. If you don't want to go out to eat in a guest room in the scenic area, you can also order takeout, which is also very convenient. In a word, this trip to Gucheng Bay felt the sincerity of the hotel in the hot summer, especially the service of Mr. Yong Wancheng, thank you very much.
